             <div class="collapsible-content__inner rte">
              <p class="p1">
               <span class="s1">
                <i>
                 Shipping Questions:
                </i>
               </span>
              </p>
              <p>
               <b>
               </b>
               <b>
                How long does shipping take?
               </b>
              </p>
              <p>
               All orders take between 2-5 business days for processing before being dispatched.
              </p>
              <p>
               *NOTE: During new releases or holidays, thereÂ may be an additional 2-4 business days of processing time.
               <span class="Apple-converted-space">
               </span>
              </p>
              <p>
               Transit times vary based upon the following conditions:
               <span class="Apple-converted-space">
               </span>
              </p>
              <ul>
               <li>
                Total distance between us and you
               </li>
               <li>
                Whether your parcel is a domestic (USA) or international shipment
               </li>
              </ul>
              <p>
              </p>
              <p>
               <b>
                How much does shipping cost:
               </b>
              </p>
              <p>
               All shipping rates will vary depending on a few different factors:
               <span class="Apple-converted-space">
               </span>
              </p>
              <ul>
               <li>
                Domestic vs. International
               </li>
               <li>
                Total weight of the package
               </li>
               <li>
                Selected shipping method
               </li>
              </ul>
              <p>
               <b>
                I entered in the incorrect address; what do I do?
               </b>
              </p>
              <p>
               Please contact us right away by going to
               <a href="https://my.amplifier.com/tools/customerservice/baaa025c-539a-4d03-b191-5998e5b9dac9">
                <strong>
                 our customer service portal
                </strong>
               </a>
               ; we begin processing orders right away but may be able to change the address if caught soon enough.
              </p>
              <p>
               <b>
                Where is my package?
                <span class="Apple-converted-space">
                </span>
               </b>
              </p>
              <p>
               Please check the associated tracking number provided in your shipment confirmation email. Any inquires on the exact location of your package should be made to the carrier directly. Our customer service agents only have as much information as can be seen by you through the tracking number.
               <span class="Apple-converted-space">
               </span>
              </p>
              <p>
               <b>
                My package was lost/stolen; what do I do?
                <span class="Apple-converted-space">
                </span>
               </b>
              </p>
              <p>
               If you feel that your package was lost or stolen, please contact the shipping carrier directly to file a claim. Once the claim is filed,
               <a href="https://my.amplifier.com/tools/customerservice/baaa025c-539a-4d03-b191-5998e5b9dac9">
                <strong>
                 please go to our customer service portal to contact us
                </strong>
               </a>
               .
              </p>
              <p>
               <b>
                Am I responsible for international duties and taxes?
                <span class="Apple-converted-space">
                </span>
               </b>
              </p>
              <p>
               Orders placed on
               <strong>
                <a href="smosh.com">
                 smosh.com
                </a>
               </strong>
               ship from the US, and allÂ international shipmentsÂ are subject to your country's applicable duties, taxes and other clearance charges.Â For international shipments, the shippingÂ charge at checkout covers the cost of freight only and does not include any applicable duties, taxes or clearance fees.
              </p>
              <p>
               <strong>
               </strong>
              </p>
              <p>
               <span>
                <i>
                 Ordering Questions:
                </i>
               </span>
              </p>
              <p>
               <b>
                Can I make changes to my order after I purchase?
                <span class="Apple-converted-space">
                </span>
               </b>
              </p>
              <p>
               We begin processing orders immediately upon receipt. For this reason, we will not be able to cancel or change your order once itâs submitted. If you decide you do not want the merchandise, you can return your order by mail.
               <span class="Apple-converted-space">
               </span>
              </p>
              <p>
               <b>
                What if an item I order goes out of stock?
               </b>
              </p>
              <p>
               If an item goes out of stock after your order is submitted, you will receive an email confirmation that youâve been refunded. You will only be charged for items that ship.
               <span class="Apple-converted-space">
               </span>
              </p>
              <p>
               <span>
                <i>
                 Returns:
                </i>
               </span>
              </p>
              <p>
               <b>
                How do I make a return?
               </b>
              </p>
              <p>
               Please use the following returns portal to contact customer service, who will assist you in starting the return.
              </p>
              <p>
               <a href="smosh.com/help">
                <strong>
                 smosh.com/help
                </strong>
               </a>
              </p>
              <p>
               <a href="https://smoshstore.returnly.com/">
                <strong>
                </strong>
               </a>
               <b>
                We do not currently accept returns for international orders.
               </b>
              </p>
              <p>
               <b>
                Although we hope to implement this soon, atÂ this time, we're unable to accept exchange requests.
               </b>
              </p>
              <meta charset="utf-8"/>
              <p>
               <span>
                Return requests must be made within 45 days of order shipped date. Items must be unworn, unwashed and still include original tags and packaging.Â We do not accept returns for any item that states "No Returns" on the description page.
               </span>
              </p>

                    <span class="s1">
                     <i>
                      Shipping Questions:
                     </i>
                    </span>
                   </p>
                   <p>
                    <b>
                    </b>
                    <b>
                     How long does shipping take?
                    </b>
                   </p>
                   <p>
                    All orders take between 2-5 business days for processing before being dispatched.
                   </p>
                   <p>
                    *NOTE: During new releases or holidays, thereÂ may be an additional 2-4 business days of processing time.
                    <span class="Apple-converted-space">
                    </span>
                   </p>
                   <p>
                    Transit times vary based upon the following conditions:
                    <span class="Apple-converted-space">
                    </span>
                   </p>
                   <ul>
                    <li>
                     Total distance between us and you
                    </li>
                    <li>
                     Whether your parcel is a domestic (USA) or international shipment
                    </li>
                   </ul>
                   <p>
                   </p>
                   <p>
                    <b>
                     How much does shipping cost:
                    </b>
                   </p>
                   <p>
                    All shipping rates will vary depending on a few different factors:
                    <span class="Apple-converted-space">
                    </span>
                   </p>
                   <ul>
                    <li>
                     Domestic vs. International
                    </li>
                    <li>
                     Total weight of the package
                    </li>
                    <li>
                     Selected shipping method
                    </li>
                   </ul>
                   <p>
                    <b>
                     I entered in the incorrect address; what do I do?
                    </b>
                   </p>
                   <p>
                    Please contact us right away by going to
                    <a href="https://my.amplifier.com/tools/customerservice/baaa025c-539a-4d03-b191-5998e5b9dac9">
                     <strong>
                      our customer service portal
                     </strong>
                    </a>
                    ; we begin processing orders right away but may be able to change the address if caught soon enough.
                   </p>
                   <p>
                    <b>
                     Where is my package?
                     <span class="Apple-converted-space">
                     </span>
                    </b>
                   </p>
                   <p>
                    Please check the associated tracking number provided in your shipment confirmation email. Any inquires on the exact location of your package should be made to the carrier directly. Our customer service agents only have as much information as can be seen by you through the tracking number.
                    <span class="Apple-converted-space">
                    </span>
                   </p>
                   <p>
                    <b>
                     My package was lost/stolen; what do I do?
                     <span class="Apple-converted-space">
                     </span>
                    </b>
                   </p>
                   <p>
                    If you feel that your package was lost or stolen, please contact the shipping carrier directly to file a claim. Once the claim is filed,
                    <a href="https://my.amplifier.com/tools/customerservice/baaa025c-539a-4d03-b191-5998e5b9dac9">
                     <strong>
                      please go to our customer service portal to contact us
                     </strong>
                    </a>
                    .
                   </p>
                   <p>
                    <b>
                     Am I responsible for international duties and taxes?
                     <span class="Apple-converted-space">
                     </span>
                    </b>
                   </p>
                   <p>
                    Orders placed on
                    <strong>
                     <a href="smosh.com">
                      smosh.com
                     </a>
                    </strong>
                    ship from the US, and allÂ international shipmentsÂ are subject to your country's applicable duties, taxes and other clearance charges.Â For international shipments, the shippingÂ charge at checkout covers the cost of freight only and does not include any applicable duties, taxes or clearance fees.
                   </p>
                   <p>
                    <strong>

                   </p>
                   <p>
                    <span>
                     <i>
                      Ordering Questions:
                     </i>
                    </span>
                   </p>
                   <p>
                    <b>
                     Can I make changes to my order after I purchase?
                     <span class="Apple-converted-space">
                     </span>
                    </b>
                   </p>

                    We begin processing orders immediately upon receipt. For this reason, we will not be able to cancel or change your order once itâs submitted. If you decide you do not want the merchandise, you can return your order by mail.

            <button aria-controls="Product-content-2-1614361364f3a851c9" class="label collapsible-trigger collapsible-trigger-btn collapsible-trigger-btn--borders" type="button">
             FAQ
             <span class="collapsible-trigger__icon collapsible-trigger__icon--open" role="presentation">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="icon icon--wide icon-chevron-down" focusable="false" role="presentation" viewbox="0 0 28 16">
               <path d="M1.57 1.59l12.76 12.77L27.1 1.59" fill="none" fill-rule="evenodd" stroke="#000" stroke-width="2">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </span>

            <div class="collapsible-content collapsible-content--all" id="Product-content-2-1614361364f3a851c9">
             <div class="collapsible-content__inner rte">
              <p class="p1">
               <span class="s1">
                <i>
                 Shipping Questions:
                </i>
               </span>
              </p>
              <p>
               <b>
               </b>
               <b>
                How long does shipping take?
               </b>
              </p>
              <p>
               All orders take between 2-5 business days for processing before being dispatched.
              </p>
              <p>
               *NOTE: During new releases or holidays, thereÂ may be an additional 2-4 business days of processing time.
               <span class="Apple-converted-space">
               </span>
              </p>
              <p>
               Transit times vary based upon the following conditions:
               <span class="Apple-converted-space">
               </span>
              </p>
              <ul>
               <li>
                Total distance between us and you
               </li>
               <li>
                Whether your parcel is a domestic (USA) or international shipment
               </li>
              </ul>
              <p>
              </p>
              <p>
               <b>
                How much does shipping cost:
               </b>
              </p>
              <p>
               All shipping rates will vary depending on a few different factors:
               <span class="Apple-converted-space">
               </span>
              </p>
              <ul>
               <li>
                Domestic vs. International
               </li>
               <li>
                Total weight of the package
               </li>
               <li>
                Selected shipping method
               </li>
              </ul>
              <p>
               <b>
                I entered in the incorrect address; what do I do?
               </b>
              </p>
              <p>
               Please contact us right away by going to
               <a href="https://my.amplifier.com/tools/customerservice/baaa025c-539a-4d03-b191-5998e5b9dac9">
                <strong>
                 our customer service portal
                </strong>
               </a>
               ; we begin processing orders right away but may be able to change the address if caught soon enough.
              </p>
              <p>
               <b>
                Where is my package?
                <span class="Apple-converted-space">
                </span>
               </b>
              </p>
              <p>
               Please check the associated tracking number provided in your shipment confirmation email. Any inquires on the exact location of your package should be made to the carrier directly. Our customer service agents only have as much information as can be seen by you through the tracking number.
               <span class="Apple-converted-space">
               </span>
              </p>
              <p>
               <b>
                My package was lost/stolen; what do I do?
                <span class="Apple-converted-space">
                </span>
               </b>
              </p>
              <p>
               If you feel that your package was lost or stolen, please contact the shipping carrier directly to file a claim. Once the claim is filed,
               <a href="https://my.amplifier.com/tools/customerservice/baaa025c-539a-4d03-b191-5998e5b9dac9">
                <strong>
                 please go to our customer service portal to contact us
                </strong>
               </a>
               .
              </p>
              <p>
               <b>
                Am I responsible for international duties and taxes?
                <span class="Apple-converted-space">
                </span>
               </b>
              </p>
              <p>
               Orders placed on
               <strong>
                <a href="smosh.com">
                 smosh.com
                </a>
               </strong>
               ship from the US, and allÂ international shipmentsÂ are subject to your country's applicable duties, taxes and other clearance charges.Â For international shipments, the shippingÂ charge at checkout covers the cost of freight only and does not include any applicable duties, taxes or clearance fees.
              </p>
              <p>
               <strong>
               </strong>
              </p>
              <p>
               <span>
                <i>
                 Ordering Questions:
                </i>
               </span>
              </p>
              <p>
               <b>
                Can I make changes to my order after I purchase?
                <span class="Apple-converted-space">
                </span>
               </b>
              </p>
              <p>
               We begin processing orders immediately upon receipt. For this reason, we will not be able to cancel or change your order once itâs submitted. If you decide you do not want the merchandise, you can return your order by mail.
               <span class="Apple-converted-space">
               </span>
              </p>
              <p>
               <b>
                What if an item I order goes out of stock?
               </b>
              </p>
              <p>
               If an item goes out of stock after your order is submitted, you will receive an email confirmation that youâve been refunded. You will only be charged for items that ship.
               <span class="Apple-converted-space">
               </span>
              </p>
              <p>
               <span>
                <i>
                 Returns:
                </i>
               </span>
              </p>
              <p>
               <b>
                How do I make a return?
               </b>
              </p>
              <p>
               Please use the following returns portal to contact customer service, who will assist you in starting the return.
              </p>
              <p>
               <a href="smosh.com/help">
                <strong>
                 smosh.com/help
                </strong>
               </a>
              </p>
              <p>
               <a href="https://smoshstore.returnly.com/">
                <strong>
                </strong>
               </a>
               <b>
                We do not currently accept returns for international orders.
               </b>
              </p>
              <p>
               <b>
                Although we hope to implement this soon, atÂ this time, we're unable to accept exchange requests.
               </b>
              </p>
              <meta charset="utf-8"/>
              <p>
               <span>
                Return requests must be made within 45 days of order shipped date. Items must be unworn, unwashed and still include original tags and packaging.Â We do not accept returns for any item that states "No Returns" on the description page.
               </span>
              </p>
             </div>
            </div>
           </div>
